Tenants of Xicheng Lane in the French Concession Establish a Citizens' Branch 195

Opposing Landlords' Illegal Contracts

Resolution to Conduct Rent Reduction Movement

Tenants of Xicheng Lane on Rue Massenet in the French Concession, at 3:00 PM yesterday, in order to oppose the landlords' harsh contracts, coercive collection of rent, and to conduct a rent reduction movement, held a general meeting of all tenants at the Fourth District Municipal Federation of Anxin Temple on Rue Albert, officially establishing the Xicheng Lane Branch of the Fourth District Municipal Federation Citizens' Association. Over a hundred tenants attended. The Fourth District Branch sent Tong Lizhang to guide the meeting. Yao Xingyuan, Zhang Xingren, and Weng Jijun were publicly elected as the presidium. Following formal protocol, Chairman Yao Xingyuan first reported the purpose of the meeting and the landlords' coercive contracts, oppressive rent collection, and the process of sealing up tenants' houses. Resolutions were made as follows: (1) Elect Ke Shenji, Zhu Bingquan, Zhang Jiayu, Gu Fujun, Yao Xingyuan, Fan Yu, Zhang Xingren, Weng Jijun, He Ming'e, Ren Xiangji, Huang Shanqing and eleven others as executive committee members to be responsible for handling the association's affairs. (2) Publish a declaration opposing the landlords' oppression. (3) Unanimously deny the illegal contract and notify everyone not to sign privately or pay rent. (4) Send a letter to the landlord stating that the terms of the contract are harsh and difficult to accept, and request that they consider the economic downturn and abide by the rent reduction methods decided by the Shanghai Rent Reduction Association to reduce rents. (5) Refer the matter to the upper-level authorities for negotiation and the branch will send a letter to the authorities requesting the prohibition of the harsh contracts. (6) Before this case is resolved, all rent should be deposited in the Bank of Communications to prevent the landlord from using it as an excuse. (7) Defer the hiring of a lawyer as a legal advisor and take legal action and demand compensation. (8) Establish a collective tenant agreement to be followed unanimously. Any violation should be considered a public enemy and punished by public deliberation. (9) Demand the replacement of the rent collector to reassure the tenants. After all the resolutions were made, the meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

Reading Q&A

Reading Guidance: Preliminary Reading of Social Sciences (II) 208

1. Regarding asking friends for advice, "Because they are influenced by the academic theories of various social science schools in contemporary society, and their views are inconsistent, the books they recommend are also different." This is not surprising. This is not only because they are influenced by academic schools, but also because their future social life determines which academic school they accept and which academic school they __. At that time, you yourself are the same. Do you like to eat sweet or salty? This depends on your taste. No matter how eloquently others speak, you will not believe them, so-called "the more they explain, the more confused I become." However, you __ have not tasted the flavors of various things clearly. If you have a little ability to distinguish, you will not make this sigh. (Regarding recognizing correct theories and distinguishing the authenticity of academic schools, please refer to the penultimate paragraph of the article "The Dispute of Theories and the Grasp of Correct Theories" in the January 10th issue of this column. I will not repeat it here.)

2. Your friend's suggestion that you first "clarify economics" is generally correct. Economics is the central science of social sciences. However, I don't know your level well, so whether this answer is applicable to you seems to still be a question. If you simply don't even have the basic knowledge of an overview of social sciences, it will be very difficult to study economics immediately. Before studying economics, you naturally need to do some preparatory work. You should have some basic knowledge of materialist dialectics and be familiar with some of the situations on the main aspects of economic phenomena. Otherwise, the methods used in economics will make you even more dizzy and confused. After reading the problems discussed inside, you will inevitably feel dry and tasteless. You don't understand the methodology of economics, you don't understand the logical order of economic research, you can't understand its mysteries, let alone feel it is dry and tasteless?

At the same time, the reading order proposed by your friend is also open to discussion. For example, it is correct to clarify economics and then study law and politics, but it is simply a logical inversion to list history and geography as the last things to read. History and geography are necessary knowledge before reading social sciences and are a means of studying social sciences. It should be placed at the beginning to be reasonable.

3. If we are talking about readers who have not yet entered the door of social sciences, we feel that the reading order should be changed to: first read a world history and one or two volumes of Chinese and foreign geography. Slightly prepare some historical and geographical knowledge. Then start reading a book on the overview of social sciences to slightly know a little about the overall concept of social sciences. Continue to read preliminary books on economics and gradually make an in-depth study of this subject. When you have a basic knowledge of economics, then go on to study what is law, what is the state, what is morality, what is art, etc. This is a path.

This path is logically correct, but human life sometimes deliberately violates logic. Some people only like to listen to sweet songs, but can't understand the tune of "Yangchun White Snow." What can be done about that? There are really many people who linger in front of the door of social sciences and then avoid it. They are afraid of the difficulty, "It's too dry and tasteless!", but they don't have a way to overcome this difficulty. The bitterness of those who retreat is, of course, a greater failure on the part of the educators. We should overcome this "difficulty", so I now propose another path.

This path is specially opened for people who stand in front of the door of social sciences and are afraid of difficulties and cannot enter. Anyone who has already entered the hall, you can continue to move forward, don't turn around and change your journey!

This path is quite easy to walk. Even people who usually only like to read novels can definitely not feel dry and tasteless or too strenuous if they follow this path, and they can still reach the hall of social sciences in the same way.

First of all, the readings we choose are soft "biographies," that is, first read the biographies of first-class social scientists, revolutionaries, etc. Biographies not only give you literary interest, but also give you methods for studying social sciences, show you how difficult it should be to do scholarship, increase your courage to self-study, defeat and shame your own cowardice, and make your people unknowingly assimilated and responded to. Imperceptibly, you will no longer find the word "difficult" in your dictionary.

Continue with "biographies," then read a history of revolution. This is a very lively book. After reading it, you will want to read more. In the meantime, you can also learn a little about the past changes of mankind, gain a lot of experience, and enlighten you on the future of mankind. This is also a book that general people should read.

After this, you can first read a book on the outline of social problems, know a little about what has happened in contemporary society; read a history of social movements to know what people in the past and present are planning to solve these social problems. Then you read a history of social evolution, know some of the laws of social evolution, and at this time, you must feel dissatisfied. Although you know many historical facts, you lack the ability to explore the causal laws of these historical facts, and you naturally want to make more fundamental research. If you really have the determination, then turn around and browse one or two books on the outline of social sciences. At the same time, attack philosophy (referring to __ materialist dialectics) and economics. In philosophy, you can acquire not only methods for studying economics, but also means for understanding the entire universe and society. In economics, naturally what you acquire should be all the knowledge for dissecting the economic structure of capitalist society. (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn

The Irrationality of Shanghai 210

— Satire

Modern people, when speaking, naturally have to bring some modern flavor, so new terms such as "economic downturn," "scientification," and "rationalization" often flow on the lips of those modern men and women, especially in Shanghai, where they can be heard everywhere. However, we look at everything in Shanghai society with a cold eye, but it is the most irrational, the most unscientific, and the exposure of the economic downturn is also the most obvious!

Let's put aside unscientificality and the economic downturn for the time being, and simply analyze all the irrational situations in Shanghai:

For example, abolishing the lunar New Year, in principle, a place like Shanghai, with its culture open and soaked in foreign atmosphere, should be very deserted. However, the facts are exactly the opposite. Gun-like firecrackers have been set off for six or seven days, and have not stopped yet. Game halls, theaters, and hotels are also announcing that they are full every day. All kinds of hustle and bustle are several times more than in the inland. On the road, young men in Western suits are cupping their hands, and doctoral gentlemen who have returned from abroad are shouting congratulations. In the Hong Temple, there are modern ladies who often appear in the Paramount dance hall burning incense...

Also, Shanghai is known as the source of Chinese culture. Many national and private universities have opened. The Shen Bao and Xinwen Bao distributed from Wangping Street travel all over the place and can almost be called representative newspapers of China. In principle, the interest of Shanghai people in reading books and newspapers must be very strong. However, as far as I know, Shanghai is full of football fans, theater fans, opium addicts, and gamblers, but it lacks "bookworms"! A large discount from a bookstore allows you to buy three and a half pounds of new books for one dollar. When a bookstore closed for the New Year, it sold brand-new literary books to its counterparts for five yuan a load. The counterparts bought them, and also said they were looking at their boss's face!

Also, the Children's National Goods Year, the Women's National Goods Year, and the ×× National Goods Promotion Week have been going on in Shanghai for almost the whole year. So, needless to say, no one buys Japanese goods at all. However, the facts tell us that the best market for Japanese goods is still Shanghai!

Also, there are the most foreign firms in Shanghai, the most comrades in Western suits in Shanghai, and Shanghai people speak the most foreign languages. In principle, all old-fashioned things in China should have been eliminated without a trace in Shanghai. However, Shanghai people are the most superstitious. Those who break down characters can make a fortune in Shanghai, and the income of the City God Temple, Jing'an Temple, and Hong Temple can exceed the income of a county government in the interior by several times or more. Moreover, many of those who donate enthusiastically are people who have received higher education and great thinkers who write articles every day advocating social reform!

Of course, the irrational phenomena in Shanghai are by no means limited to the few points I have listed above. Fortunately, most of them are extremely obvious, so I don't need to write much more.

Odds and Ends After a Thorough Cleaning 211

—

The same time, the same month and day, when the lunar year comes to an end, there is naturally an unspeakable busyness. Even families are doing all kinds of silly things that bother people, such as "sending off the Kitchen God," "thorough cleaning," "thanking the gods," and "staying up all night." The officialdom prohibits it on its own, and each family holds it as usual.

Among the things done at the end of the year, "thorough cleaning" is relatively interesting. Because there is always a lot of dust, dirt and rubbish in a house. Although it is also cleaned daily, there may be some imperfections. At the end of the year, a big clean-up is done, sweeping away cobwebs, rat droppings, broken bottles, and broken bowls. If you change it to a new term, it is "cleaning movement," isn't it nice and fashionable!

Cleaning the house a little, it always feels more comfortable. Let's take an individual as an example. If one is covered in sores and scabs, and it is uncomfortable to scratch, how comfortable it is to soak in a scalding pool. The prisoners in prison are covered with lice and dirt. Once they get out of prison, they hurry to shave their heads and take a bath, and then __ regain __ health. The meaning of this "thorough cleaning" is __ __ what I said on the side.

But __ can __ only __ clean the filth in the house, but what about cleaning the __ on the body, and the inner foulness, danger, greed, meanness, depravity, and obscenity? I don't know what method can be used to clean them all away. Even though medicine is developed, the syphilis virus can be injected with 606; the rotting of the throat tube can be injected with serum. Only the virus and rot in the heart cannot be thought of.

Looking at the world stage, there are many places where war clouds are thick; there are many places where there is unemployment and panic; there are also political instability, and there are also social downturns. Can all of these be swept away? To see it smaller, in the society we are in, there is opium, gambling, trading, kidnapping, robbery, rape... Can these many stains be swept away?

Cleaning, cleaning, after all, is just a nice word for people to beautify their faces. You can sweep away the filth on the outside, but can you sweep away the foulness in the heart?

Odds and Ends 212

— Yu Youqing

Guiyou is the year of the Rooster, and Jiaxu is the year of the Dog, which is exactly the same as the Rooster and Dog living beings, making them disturbed and unbearable. Our China may be as pitiful as Rooster and Dog scraps.

Originally, the Rooster has five virtues, and the Dog has righteousness. They are both domestic animals loved by people, but when the Rooster flies on the roof, and the Dog cries at night, people think it is unlucky. However, thanks to Lord Mengchang, it was only because of the diners who crowed like roosters and stole like dogs that he was able to safely escape Hangu Pass.

"A hen crowing at dawn" is used to describe a woman in power, which is inherently inappropriate. Because in the past, women were always subjugated to men and made playthings. It has not changed for thousands of years, but it is not right now. The call for raising women's rights and liberating men and women is getting higher and higher. Almost all men are now turned into servants of dressing tables. Perhaps the hen crowing at dawn has become a reality!

"The Shu dog barks at the sun" is also an exaggerated phrase. Literally, dogs in Sichuan bark wildly when they see the sun. Because Sichuan has many mountains and it is difficult to see the sun, the Shu dogs bark wildly when they see the sun. This means that sitting in a well and looking at the sky, what you see is small. Maybe Shanghai people say that people from other places lack sophistication, calling them diehards. However, if you drop a literary phrase, you can also say that it is the Shu dog barking at the sun.

"Chickens and dogs ascend to heaven" means that everyone enjoys the benefits of one person's good fortune. Nowadays, many people in authority, once they get their way, then his father's party, mother's party, and wife's party, these three parties can rely on him alone to enjoy happiness. What a lucky thing this is! So, if a commoner wants to get ahead, may I ask if he has a maternal uncle or brother-in-law who is a big tycoon? Alas! Needless to say.

Radio News 213

— Wonderful God

Recently, radio stations can be described as flourishing. However, the wavelengths used are mostly in the longwave range. And the power, apart from the Central Broadcasting Station, was originally no more than 500 watts. Therefore, the broadcasting range only reached the southeastern provinces. Now, the local International Radio Station has built a new shortwave broadcasting station, with a massive power of 25,000 watts. Its broadcasting range can reach the entire world. It is said that during the trial broadcasting the other day, a report from London stated that the sound was clear and loud, and the effect was excellent.

Few outsiders know the content of this station. At the invitation of the station's engineer, I once went to visit the broadcasting room. I found the decoration magnificent, unmatched by any broadcasting room on the sea. The broadcasting machine and all other components are produced by the British Marconi Company. The broadcasting machine is located in Zhenru, and the broadcasting room is located in the Sassoon Building in the city. Remote control is used for communication. I only visited the broadcasting room; I didn't go to the Zhenru machine because it was too far. The broadcasting room fully adopts the decoration of an Oriental palace, and also takes into account artistic patterns. The roof is decorated with gold and red, and embellished with golden dragons, etc. The four walls are all decorated with calligraphy and paintings, embedded on the walls. The layout method is unique and not purely Oriental. Because it is in a steel-concrete building, many scientific facilities are also used. When broadcasting, in order to avoid echoes, the four walls are covered with velvet, and the floor is covered with extremely thick carpets. It is said that the velvet and carpets alone cost more than 3,000 yuan. The electric lights in the broadcasting room are shaped like palace lanterns and are entirely made of glass, which are quite beautiful.

Recently, trial broadcasts are often conducted from 8 or 9 pm every night, with a wavelength of 26 meters. Formal broadcasting will begin on February 3. However, this station is not entirely for entertainment purposes. If this city wants to talk to London, it only needs to pay a considerable fee, and it can be done. It is essentially a commercial long-distance wireless telephone.

Four Northeast Company Commanders 214

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Four

Drinking Wine and Passing Dishes, Merrymaking with Tears of Farewell

Lighting a Lamp, Dreaming of Low Singing, Passing a Long Night

Guizhi smiled and said, "There are only two taels of wine in total, and you drank half a cup in one gulp. Are we just going to eat vegetables from now on? You probably haven't heard me sing ditties yet. Let me sing a little bit for you." Ziqiang smiled and looked at him, saying, "You can sing? I really didn't know that. What kind of ditty can you sing?" Guizhi twisted his head with a smile and said, "I can sing a few, but I'm afraid the old man will hear me and scold me." Ziqiang smiled and said, "Just sing softly, it's okay. You and I sit hugging the corner of the table. Anyway, no matter how low you sing, I can hear you." Guizhi picked up the wine cup and smelled it, pretending to want to drink it. But as soon as it got close to his mouth, he put the wine cup down again, smiled, and said, "I won't sing. I don't sing well, and you'll laugh at me." Ziqiang saw that he wanted to sing, but he was also afraid to sing. He didn't know how to say it properly. So he picked up the cup and just smiled at him. At this moment, the distant sound of the night watchman, along with the wind, was sent into his ears. Guizhi搶着 (搶着, not "snatching" but "taking the initiative to" or "quickly") smiled and said, "I'll sing anyway. But ditties are not elegant. I'll sing a big opera for you, okay?" Ziqiang smiled and said, "You can sing big opera too? That's even better. What role do you sing?" Guizhi smiled and said, "Everything is a mess. I can sing a few lines of anything. My best is 'Yang Guifei Gets Drunk.'" Ziqiang stretched a hand over from the corner of the table and gently patted the back of his hand, saying, "This opera is very good. Just sing this one. Besides, I'm already drunk." Guizhi, hearing this, really coughed lightly twice, and then, with a smile, began to sing softly. While he sang, he listened to the outside, listening to the sound of the night watchman on the street, to see if it was far away. Only when he couldn't hear the sound of the night watchman at all did he stop singing. (318)

Local Customs Anecdotes

Suzhou at the End of the Abolished Lunar Year 215

— Wu Men Shayu

Our country is indeed a country that preserves the old. Although the lunar calendar has been abolished to this day, customs and habits are still deeply rooted and difficult to change. The sound of firecrackers and the clamor of drums create a scene of peace and prosperity. In Suzhou, at the end of the abolished lunar year, of course there are many "old rules of the year" that are carried out according to precedent. Writing them out now is also a kind of local custom anecdote.

Burning First Incense

Although the government has repeatedly issued orders and expressly prohibited superstitious acts of worshiping Buddha and burning incense, those who prohibit do so, and those who do it do so. It has long become a mere formality on paper. In Suzhou, where incense is very popular, not to mention old-fashioned women, even modern girls and intellectuals are prostrating and worshiping under the idols in the county. At midnight, when New Year's Eve and New Year's Day meet, in the Sanqing Hall of Yuanmiao Temple, in front of the sixty star deities, candlelight is already flickering, and incense is wafting. Many pious men and women are worshiping and rising and falling. According to popular custom, the earlier this star incense is burned, the sooner one can get blessings and prosperity at the beginning of the year. Therefore, a group of people who want to have good luck early sit and wait for dawn, rushing to burn the first incense. Especially the courtesans of the northern districts, come in convoys of cars, with the fragrance of rouge and powder, intermingling with the incense and red candles in the hall, forming a rich atmosphere.

Circulating in the Auspicious Direction

Everyone likes to seek good fortune. Those bright and understanding gentlemen need to seek good fortune and avoid evil even more. Therefore, on New Year's Day, the first day of the new year, they must first check the almanac to see which direction the God of Joy is in and which direction the God of Wealth is in. Then they go out the door and follow those directions. There are still many people who circulate in the auspicious direction in modern times.

Olive Tea

Although colorful banknotes are now popular, and silver dollars are also being naturally eliminated according to the law, the people still support and worship yuanbao (元寶, silver ingots) from beginning to end. When it comes to the end of the year, the year cake is made into yuanbao, the olive is called yuanbao, and the dishes with yuanbao are countless. The society is full of the sound of "yuanbao". At the end of the abolished lunar year, two olives are added to each pot of red tea in Suzhou's teahouses, called "yuanbao tea," to please the tea guests. This custom has been followed for a long time and is still practiced today.

Welcoming the God of Wealth

The God of Wealth is just the God of Wealth. According to the "Investiture of the Gods," when Taigong Wang was on the Investiture of the Gods platform, he invested five Gods of Wealth, who were in charge of human wealth. This absurd mythology is depicted in divine scrolls and deeply imprinted in the minds of the people, especially a group of merchants who value profit, who hope to bring the God of Wealth into the store so that their profits will be great. Therefore, on the fifth day of the first lunar month, homes and shops prepare large pieces of meat, whole chickens, and whole catfish, and welcome the God of Wealth with gongs and drums. After the shopkeepers welcome the God of Wealth, they make a feast of the fish and meat used to welcome the God of Wealth, calling it the God of Wealth wine, and then open for business and resume business.

Lighting and Extinguishing the Lamps 216

The lamps are lit on the thirteenth day and extinguished on the eighteenth day. According to Suzhou custom, on the night of the thirteenth, red candles must be lit in front of the enshrined divine scroll in the hall, called "lighting the lamps," and they are lit every night from the thirteenth to the eighteenth. After the eighteenth, the divine scroll is put away and the New Year's scene is cleaned up. On the nights of lighting and extinguishing the lamps, glutinous rice balls and round cakes must also be offered in front of the divine scroll. During these days, in Suzhou's Song Xianzhou Lane Mengjiang Hall, candles as thick as arms are burned in front of the gods, and red men and green women go in groups, which is very lively, called watching "big candles." At night, there are also firecrackers to add to the fun.

In addition to the above items, which are customarily followed, Suzhou's New Year's customs also include the fashion of riding in horse-drawn carriages on Jinlü Road during the New Year. A group of carefree friends holding flowers gallop back and forth on the road to show off their wealth. In recent years, the flower market has been depressed, and cinemas have flourished, and riding in horse-drawn carriages has been eliminated invisibly.

Brief News 217

The Suzhou YMCA will hold an exhibition of more than 200 recent works by the famous painter Tao Lengyue starting on February 18, lasting for seven days. At each of Tao's past painting exhibitions, celebrities from home and abroad have spared no expense to seek his works, and his reputation has spread throughout the art world. Tao has served as a professor at various universities, and his footprints have covered half the world, so his paintings have been aided by famous mountains and great rivers, and are strange, majestic, and extraordinary. Last autumn, he accepted an invitation to teach at Sichuan University, entered Sichuan for a tour, and this spring, he went east again to climb Mount Heng to explore the scenery, and the smoke and clouds under his pen have become even more spectacular.

The Fifth China Central Games is Scheduled to be Held in Wuhan 220

The Hubei Provincial Government Approves the Establishment of a Preparatory Committee

Immediately Notify All Provinces to Prepare to Participate

Hankou Correspondence, The Fifth China Central Games, originally scheduled to be held in Wuhan in the 20th year of the Republic of China, was to be prepared by the former Hankou Special City Education Bureau. Later, Hankou City was transferred to the Hubei Provincial Government, and the association was taken over by the Jiaoyu Hall. A preparatory committee was immediately established, and a budget was prepared, including the conference period expenses and repairs to the public sports field, totaling more than 37,700 yuan in national currency. It was submitted to the provincial government meeting for approval. At that time, due to the severe flood disaster, it was ordered to be postponed to the spring of 丨year. The event was again postponed for one year, and the General Headquarters for Bandit Suppression in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces ordered a temporary postponement. As a result, the conference has been postponed for more than three years. Cheng Qibao, the director of the Jiaoyu Hall, believes that developing national sports and holding competitions in conjunction with the provinces of Central China should not be delayed any longer. On the 15th, a meeting was convened to decide to hold the games in mid-May. According to Article 7, Section 6 of the Charter of the China Central Sports Federation, a preparatory office should be organized one month before the games, and all provinces should be notified to prepare to participate. Now that the deadline is approaching, a preparatory committee should be quickly formed to plan and proceed. Regarding funding, in addition to the preparatory expenses, sports field repair expenses, conference period expenses, and expenses for the province's athletes, which should be paid by the province, the travel, food, and other miscellaneous expenses for athletes and staff from other units will be borne by the units themselves to save money. As for the venue, both Wuchang and Hankou are suitable. However, Wuchang is the provincial capital, and there are many schools, so more athletes can participate. The Provincial Public Sports Field has hosted the Third National Games and the Seventh National Football Regional Games, and the scale is roughly complete and easier to repair. Therefore, the above methods were proposed as a proposal to the Provincial Government's regular meeting on the 20th. After discussion, it was resolved to approve the establishment of a preparatory committee. The sports venue will be determined according to the equipment conditions of the sports fields in Wuhan, and the required expenses will be budgeted by the Jiaoyu Hall and submitted for approval. The Defendant in the Case of Injury to a Referee Did Not Appear and the Hearing Was Postponed 221

Shanghai sports referee Shen Huichun served as a referee at the Jiaotong University Stadium on the afternoon of December 16 last year. The game was a football match between Jiaotong University and Jinan University. As a result, Jiaotong University lost by one goal. Jiaotong University students Qin Shaoji and others blamed the referee for being unfair and surrounded Shen to make things difficult, and even beat Shen. After Shen Huichun went to the local court to request an examination of the injuries, prosecutor Tang Ruxiu confirmed that Shen was indeed injured and prosecuted the case to the criminal court. A public hearing was scheduled for the 21st of this month. The details have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the case was due yesterday. At 10:00 a.m., Shen Huichun and his lawyer, E Sen, reported to the court. Subsequently, Judge Guan Liting specially opened the thirteenth court for trial. Shen and lawyer E attended the court at the same time. After the judge briefly questioned Shen, he said that the defendant Qin Shaoji had not arrived today and had submitted a petition requesting a postponement. The hearing would be rescheduled after another date was set. The court was then adjourned.

Report on the Inspection of Physical Education Supervisors of the Ministry of Education Has Been Submitted to the Ministry 230

Hao Lisheng, a physical education supervisor of the Ministry of Education, recently inspected five schools in Shanghai: Dongya Technical College, Patriotic Women's Physical Education Department, Southeast Sports Teacher Training School, Liangjiang Sports Teacher Training School, and China Sports Teacher Training School. The inspection reports for each school have listed the points that should be promoted and reformed, and there are concrete improvement measures. The reports have been submitted to the Minister for review. The Minister of Education has asked the Higher and Ordinary Education Bureaus to sign their opinions, and after a certain period of time, each school will be ordered to comply.

Established in August of the 18th year (1929), it has 84 full-time staff, 24 part-time staff, and 24 researchers. The monthly expenditure is approximately 50,000 yuan. It also cooperates with other academic institutions. The institutes are divided into various departments and have made considerable achievements in research, investigation, and experimentation.

Dong Kunfan Will Go Abroad to Investigate Vocational Education 236

Dong Kunfan, a vocational education expert and director of the Fujian Hui'er Orphanage, participated in the Chicago World's Fair last year. The Ministry of Education requested that he take the opportunity to investigate vocational education in Europe and the United States. However, due to Dong's urgent need to return to China to prepare for China's participation in this year's Chicago World's Fair, he was unable to conduct the investigation. It is now learned that Dong has completed the preparations for the Chicago World's Fair and has decided to go abroad for investigation in the near future. He plans to first go to the United States, then to Europe, Soviet Russia, Japan, and other countries. The scope of the investigation will cover the administration and management of vocational education, the management of education for poor children, the vocational problems of poor children, production capacity, sales channels, and a study of the reasons why society and vocational education cannot be integrated, as well as the causes of pauperization. The investigation period is expected to be one year.

Recent Situation of Education in Guangdong and Guangxi 237

▲Summary of a Speech by Ministry of Education Counselor Chen Panzao

When the Ministry of Education held its memorial week meeting on the 19th morning, Counselor Chen Panzao presented a summary report on his inspection of the education situation in Guangdong and Guangxi. The main points are recorded below:

▲Guangdong Province (1) Number of Schools: There are a total of 356 secondary schools in the province, including 64 rural normal schools and normal schools, and 31 vocational schools. Those belonging to the provincial level include 13 middle schools, 1 girls' middle school, 1 industrial vocational school, 6 normal schools, 1 girls' normal school, 2 agricultural schools, 1 commercial school, and more than 10 kindergartens. The rest are established by various counties in Guangdong (67 out of 96 counties and cities in Guangdong have middle schools). The county with the most middle schools is Taishan, with 14 or 15 middle schools. There are a total of 19,967 county-level elementary schools in the province. Taishan County has 1,278 elementary schools. (2) Education Funding: The provincial education funding was 2.49 million last year and 2.36 million this year. It has increased by 870,000 in one year. According to the province's three-year plan, the estimated education funding for the first year (next year) is 5.46 million, the education funding for the second year is 8.44 million, and the education funding for the third year is 11.49 million. Based on the past increase in funding, this plan is not just empty talk. The future surge in education will be even more impressive. The elementary school funding for all 96 counties and cities in the province is a total of 13,405,290 yuan, of which Taishan County's elementary school funding is 1,111,878 yuan. (3) Social Education: In order to promote social education, the province has established the Guangdong Province Social Education Experimental Zone and investigated and compiled statistics on the social education carried out by various counties and cities in order to promote it. Regarding increasing funding for social education, various counties and cities have now raised it to more than 781,000 yuan. In terms of promoting mass education, in addition to establishing the Provincial Mass Education Personnel Training Institute to train teachers, it has also established a mass sports experimental zone, the Provincial Experimental Mass Education Center, and formulated measures to promote mass schools to supervise the implementation of various counties and cities. (4) Vocational Education: In order to develop vocational education, the province will transform the five provincial normal schools into the First Agricultural School, transform the Shunde County Junior High School into the First Agricultural School, prepare for the establishment of the Third Agricultural School, establish the Provincial First Vocational School, reorganize the Guangdong Commercial School, add industrial subjects to the Provincial Fourth Middle School, subsidize private middle schools to add advanced vocational subjects, handle the registration of vocational education personnel, and supervise various counties to open vocational schools in order to promote vocational education as much as possible.

▲Guangzhou City: Guangzhou City, which belongs to Guangdong Province, has nine secondary schools (Normal School, First Middle School, Second Middle School, Third Middle School, First Vocational School, Second Vocational School, Third Vocational School, Art School, Nanny School). Including public and private schools, there are a total of 83 schools. There are 4 labor, rural, and schools, Xiangqin University Schools, 93 elementary schools, more than 70 private elementary schools, more than 6 supplementary schools, 80 to 90 mass schools, and more than 10 kindergartens. There are currently more than 50,000 students in the city. Among the total population of 1,122,500 people, there are 396,900 illiterate people and more than 30,000 out-of-school children. Its vocational schools have civil service courses, Western medicine dispensing courses, typesetting and printing courses, automobile driving courses, and other applied courses. The employment prospects for graduates are still quite good. The city's educational expenditure is 1.26 million yuan. The recent educational progress of the city in recent years is as follows: In the 15th year (1926), there were 108 schools, 17,831 students, and 569,000 yuan in funding. In the 16th year (1927), there were 168 schools, 23,560 students, and 691,000 yuan in funding. In the 17th year (1928), there were 192 schools, 32,683 students, and 1,025,000 yuan in funding. In the 18th year (1929), there were 272 schools, 49,512 students, and 1,473,000 yuan in funding. In the 19th year (1930), there were 256 schools, 52,346 students, and 1,833,000 yuan in funding. The number of schools and students has increased sharply, and the funding is now 2.16 million yuan. Its rapid progress and increase in quantity are unmatched by other cities.

▲Guangxi Province (1) Number of Schools: There are 2 universities and vocational schools, 5 complete middle schools, 3 senior high schools, 56 junior high schools, 28 normal training institutes, 2 vocational schools. The total number of secondary schools is 94. There are 1,092 higher elementary schools, 11,440 lower elementary schools, 6 kindergartens, and 55 other elementary schools. The total number of primary education is 12,595 schools (among Guangxi's 94 counties, 20 to 30 counties have no middle schools, and there are only a dozen or so private middle schools). (2) Social Education Institutions: There are a total of 704 school-style mass schools, supplementary schools, and special schools. There are a total of 1,055 social-style mass education centers, libraries, gymnasiums, popular lecture halls, reading rooms, literacy stations, entertainment venues, and other social education institutions. The total number of the above is 1,759. (3) Education Funding: Higher education is 262,595 yuan, secondary education is 240,045 yuan, and primary education is 4,375,909 yuan. The total of the three items is 6,778,549 yuan. Social education funding is 406,060 yuan. (4) Total Number of Students: Universities and vocational schools have 708 people, secondary education schools have 10,750 people, and primary education schools have 545,738 people. The total of the three items is 567,206 people. (5) Military Training: The province's military training middle schools from the senior high school grade and junior high school third grade implement military training for one hour every afternoon. The training is strict, which is unmatched by other provinces. They all use the militia system for eradicating illiteracy and mass military training. In addition to teaching two hours of necessary civic courses and knowledge every day, most of the time is spent on military training. There are now hundreds of thousands of militias, who receive two hours of education every day, which greatly benefits the promotion of mass literacy education. It is also a special situation in the province. (6) Future Plans: In order to meet modern needs, the province plans to transform the middle schools in various counties into rural normal schools and vocational schools. Many provincial middle schools have now been transformed into vocational schools. In order to implement the five-year plan, it is planned to popularize compulsory education throughout the province within these five years. The National Basic Education Research Institute has been established to carry out the plan.

Local News

Independent Education Funding Committee Investigates Tax Revenue in This City 238

▲And Issues a Declaration

The Independent Education Funding Movement Committee of this city, jointly organized by the City Education Association, the Greater Education Federation, and the Education Federation, has begun working in the City Education Association since its establishment. Ma Jiazhen, Jiang Menglin, Sheng Zhensheng, and other three committee members were specially appointed to first investigate the tax revenue situation in this city as the basis for independent education funding, and issued a declaration to promote the unified progress of the education sector in the city. The organizational rules of the association have been passed at the first meeting and are attached below: (1) This association is organized by 11 to 30 committee members hired by the City Education Association, the Greater Education Federation, and the Education Federation. (2) This association holds a regular meeting once a month, and may hold temporary meetings when necessary. (3) This association must have a quorum of more than half of all committee members to hold a formal meeting. (4) This association elects seven executive committee members from among the committee members to form the executive committee to handle daily affairs. (5) The executive committee shall divide the organization and management according to the complexity of the affairs. (6) The office of this association is temporarily located in the Shanghai City Education Association, Daji Road, Nanshi. (7) This association will be dissolved after the independent education funding of this city. (8) These rules shall be implemented after being passed by the entire committee. If there are any incomplete matters, they may be proposed for amendment at the regular meeting.

The Results of the Essay Contest for Ms. Gao's Prize of the Science Society of China are Announced 239

▲Chen Guoda, a Student of Sun Yat-sen University in Guangzhou, Was Selected

Ms. Gao Junshan, a member of the Science Society of China, holds an essay contest every year to commemorate her deceased sister, Ms. Gao Junwei, a deceased member of the society. The subject of the essay contest in the 21st year was geography. The essays submitted have been reviewed by the essay contest committee, and the essay "The Problem of the Guangzhou Delta" by Chen Guoda, a student of National Sun Yat-sen University in Guangzhou, has been selected as the winning essay of the Ms. Gao Memorial Prize Essay Contest of the 11th year of the society. In addition to the society awarding US$100 and a gold award medal, his essay will be published in the society's scientific journal.

The Shanghai St. John's Alumni Association Celebrated President Bu Fangji's 70th Birthday Last Night 240

▲The Lights Were Brilliant, and More Than 400 Alumni Arrived

▲Mayor Wu and Wang Zhengting Both Attended and Gave Speeches

The Shanghai Branch of the St. John's University Alumni Association held a grand celebration last night in the Mother School's Friendship Room in Fanwangdu to celebrate the 70th birthday of President Bu Fangji. More than 400 alumni attended, making it a grand occasion for a time. The school was surrounded by colorful electric lights that were dazzling. The huge red electric "Longevity" character in front of the Friendship Room was particularly brilliant. Today, the students in the school held a celebration, including a games and other fun programs. From 4:00 pm to 6:00 pm tomorrow, guests will be received.

Those who arrived yesterday included alumni Liu Hongsheng, Wang Zhengting, Pan Gongzhan, Song Ziliang, Ma Chonggan, Chen Xing, Li Denghui, Chen Heqin, Fu Qing, Xu Shanxiang, Gu Angruo, Fan Wenzhao, Pan Xulun, Liu Lingfang, Guo Chengen, Guo Bingwen, Yuan Ludeng, Zhang Jiafu, Shen Siliang, Wang Boqi, Wang Zhongwei, Zhong Ketuo, Cai Zhenghua, Xu Naiji, Liu Linsheng, and President Bu, Mrs. Bu, all the faculty and staff, and guests Wu Tiecheng, Li Zhaohuan, and others, totaling more than 400 people. ▲Business Meeting: At 7:00 pm, a business meeting was held first. Pan Gongzhan, the president of the Alumni Association, reported on the association's affairs over the past year, and Ma Chonggan reported on the economic situation. Then, the association's affairs were discussed. Finally, the next session of officers was elected. Wu Qingtai was elected president, Huang Yiping was elected secretary, and Li Baojun was elected accountant. ▲Celebration Banquet: The celebration banquet was held at 8:00 pm, hosted by Li Moxi, Xu Shanxiang, Pan Xulun, Li Di, Yang Caiqing, Gu Angruo, and others.

▲Chairman Pan's Speech: At 8:30 pm, Chairman Pan Gongzhan delivered the opening speech, saying that today we are celebrating President Bu's 70th birthday, but he has been running St. John's University for 50 years. His contribution is very great. Fifty years ago, China was just starting to run new education. President Bu's birth seemed to be specially for China to run new education. St. John's has produced many talents who serve the society. This is all thanks to President Bu. Next, Mayor Wu gave a speech, "The Purpose of Chinese Education." Xiao Zhiji then read congratulatory telegrams from Shi Zhaoji, Yan Huiqing, and more than 30 alumni associations in New York, Beiping, Kaifeng, Nanjing, Changsha, and other places. Then, Yang Runshen represented the alumni in presenting President Bu with a large refrigerator, and Liu Hongsheng and Song Ziliang presented him with a car. All the alumni presented him with public shares worth 15,000 yuan. Then, Wang Zhengting gave a speech, congratulating President Bu on the three words of loyalty, constancy, and clarity. President Bu gave a speech, praising the cooperation of St. John's faculty, staff, students, and alumni association, which led to today's success. Finally, Cao Yunxiang talked about his memories in school. Li Denghui and Li Zhaohuan also gave speeches. Finally, alumnus Yuan Ludeng sang Peking opera, and the whole audience sang the school song and the alumni association song, which did not end until 10:30 pm. Excerpts from the speeches are as follows: It was broadcast by radio station last night at that time.

▲Mayor Wu's Speech: Today is the annual meeting of the St. John's Alumni Association, and it also happens to be the eve of President Bu's 70th birthday. Tiecheng is very honored to participate in the grand event. President Bu has devoted his energy to St. John's University for many years, and his achievements are remarkable and praised by everyone. Today, there are many students, and President Bu's teachings are like the warmth of the spring breeze. His spirit is strong, and he is old but not declining. As the saying goes, it is rare to live to seventy years old. Now President Bu's longevity has reached the age of seventy, and President Bu's direct and indirect contributions to society and the world are even rarer and more valuable in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. St. John's University has a long history in China. St. John's graduates have served in various national and social agencies for many years, not only in large numbers, but also with outstanding reputations. Such commendable and great achievements are not accidental, nor can they be expected in a short time. Of course, it is the result of President Bu and all the faculty and staff's hard work for many years and enthusiastic cultivation. We cannot but express our deep respect for President Bu and all the faculty and staff's perseverance and spirit in educating talents, and we cannot but express our ardent expectations. Education is a great force that promotes culture and drives the nation. Ancient China's governance was based on education, which produced China's beautiful culture and created China's glorious and brilliant history. However, the purpose of education must be able to adapt to the needs of the nation, and the needs of the nation should adapt to the great trend of the times. The education of a country must be built on the purpose of adapting to the great trend of the times and the needs of the nation in order to generate power, promote culture, and drive the nation. Although modern Chinese education has also undergone many reforms, it has failed to truly adapt to the great trend of the times and the needs of the nation, resulting in today's decline and an unprecedented national crisis. The narrow nationalism of education has been rejected by the great trend of the times, and it is also incompatible with the Chinese national spirit and the spirit of the Great Harmony of Wangdao. However, China's inherent beautiful culture, long history, and special and important position should not be ignored by anyone who is objectively concerned about world issues and by educators with foresight. The direction of current Chinese education, driven by the times and the environment, has shown a significant tendency to change. The spirit of this change is undoubtedly to attempt the revival of the nation, on the one hand to restore our nation's inherent ability to create culture, and on the other hand to absorb and improve its production technology. The function of this educational purpose can not only develop and enrich the power of the country, but also make a great and unlimited contribution to the future of world culture. Tonight, Tiecheng hopes to celebrate the development of St. John's with this point of view, and at the same time, to celebrate President Bu's birthday with this enthusiasm.

▲Wang Zhengting's Speech: Dr. Wang Zhengting's speech briefly stated that President Bu's morality and learning are admirable, and what makes us most admire him can be summarized in three words: loyalty, constancy, and clarity. Loyalty is connected to love. President Bu is loyal to the school and is willing to sacrifice his position and rights rather than abandon St. John's. This is why St. John's is St. John's. Confucius encouraged people to be constant. Great men and leaders in ancient and modern times can only succeed if they are constant. President Bu has worked hard day and night for 50 years. It is truly what is called decades as one day. His spirit of running the school is the second thing that can be learned from. Clarity means having a broad vision. Educators must have a broad vision. President Bu can integrate ancient and modern thoughts and cultivate talents. Education changes with the environment. President Bu was able to see the Chinese society of many years later many years ago and cultivate talents from all walks of life. St. John's alumni are all outstanding, which makes people admire him even more.

▲President Bu's Speech: President Bu Fangji's speech briefly stated that he was deeply grateful for the opportunity to come to China and create this St. John's University. The mainland newspaper reported that St. John's was founded by me alone, which is a big mistake. Therefore, secondly, St. John's success is due to the concerted efforts and cooperation of all the colleagues and faculty in the school. Moreover, the success of St. John's is due to the alumni association's loyalty to the alma mater, which is unmatched by other schools. In the rest of my life, I would like to travel to the east, west, north, and south of China, as far as Xichuan, Chengdu, and Chongqing, to visit my alumni in various places. This will be very gratifying.

Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts Officially Starts Classes 248

The Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts held its spring commencement ceremony on the 15th of this month. Student registration has been very enthusiastic recently. Acting Principal Wang Jiyuan is making various plans to promote school affairs. This term, Tang Jun has been newly hired as a professor of Art Theory, Jin Lvsheng as a professor of Music, Cao Yunzhong as a professor of Western Painting, and Wang Jichang as a professor of Traditional Painting. To integrate teaching and practice, the school has also organized a Teaching Affairs Committee and a Guidance Committee. Classes officially start today. Over sixty new students have been admitted to various departments this term. It is said that vacancies still exist in various departments, and those with aspirations are welcome to apply at any time.

Civic Education Center and Supplementary School Enrolling Students 249

The previous session of the Shanghai Municipal Civic Education Center's Civic Supplementary School has concluded as scheduled. The Education Section of the center is currently preparing for the enrollment of the next session. It is said that the new session will focus on three objectives: literacy, civic knowledge, and vocational training. The classes are divided into three levels: literacy classes, civics classes, and vocational classes, enrolling a total of 150 students. Enrollment qualifications are open to all genders, aged 16 to 50. Tuition is free, and supplies are provided by the center. The deadline for registration is the 26th, and classes will begin on March 1st.

Qualified candidates should have studied in Germany or graduated from a domestic university and have a strong command of German. Those interested should contact the association as soon as possible.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Two! A Heart! A Face! 251

— Yang An

In this era of foreign goods dominating the market and rural areas declining, everyone sees the national products industry as dim and hopeless. Those who run national products factories are frowning, believing there is no way out. While this is the reality, a closer look reveals that the future of national products is only bright, not dark; only developing, not declining. It depends on people. As long as everyone has the determination and perseverance.

Two Keys

Those running national products factories only need to grasp two keys: One is thorough cooperation, from cooperation among the same industry to cooperation between different industries. Shift from the previous mindset of jealousy and infighting to a united effort of mutual assistance in production and sales, resisting the dumping of foreign goods. The other is reducing costs. What methods can be used to reduce materials and labor while accelerating and increasing production? What records can be kept to constantly examine what is unreasonable and uneconomical, providing a basis for continuous improvement and savings? In short, the life of national products depends on everyone's efforts to improve products, not on surviving through price drops and shoddy workmanship.

A Sincere Heart

The term "Buy National Products" is almost universally known, and everyone considers it a valuable undertaking. Even the average wife, madam, and young lady believe it is a very stylish thing to do. If you don't believe it, you can visit a national products company and see that women who love using national products are just as numerous as men. However, everyone must have a sincere heart, or in other words, a sense of faith. With faith, even if the goods are slightly inferior or the prices are higher, they will be patronized because of a spirit of sacrifice.

A Smiling Face

For those who sell national products, the most important thing is a smiling face. They interact with customers who love national products every day, and their greatest effort lies in their responses, greetings, voices, smiles, and expressions. Deadpan faces and grumpy faces are not what should be seen in a national products company. If you offend one customer, you not only lose a year's worth of business but also scare away other enthusiastic customers. Losing customers is like being an enemy of national products. Therefore, if you are not going to be a clerk in a national products company, that is fine, but if you are going to be a clerk, first look at your own face.

New Year's Delight 252

— Huang Shuying

丨Discovered a New National Product丨

Throughout the year, there are two things that I find most unpleasant: One is that every time Wang Ma brings the wash water to the dressing table, when I go to wash my face, the mirror on the dressing table is always covered with a layer of fog due to the steam from the hot water. I have to wipe it three or four times with a dry cloth before I can see my reflection. I wash my face three times a day, and each time it is so annoying and unpleasant. The other is that every time I eat, as soon as I bring the bowl of rice close to me, my glasses fog up due to the steam from the rice, forcing me to take them off. However, my nearsightedness is so severe that I cannot see without my glasses. This is even more painful than the fog on the dressing table mirror. All year round, I am troubled by these two small things! "The scientific community has already invented wireless technology, why hasn't there been an invention to eliminate the annoying fog?" I often think to myself. On January 16th, I got up in the morning and was bothered by the fog again. As usual, I first flipped through the day's newspaper and then went to suffer the second round of fog. Suddenly, I caught sight of a striking advertisement stating that a Tiangong Industrial Company had invented a wonderful product to remove fog, called "Yun De Xiao." If you apply it to any glass surface, all fog will be repelled. "Is there really such an invention?" I exclaimed excitedly, and without even eating a proper breakfast, I immediately rushed to the only national products store, the China National Products Company.

As soon as I entered the China National Products Company, my eyes greedily darted around, searching for what I needed like a hungry wolf. At first, I thought that "Yun De Xiao" should be sold in the hardware department, so I went to the hardware department, but it wasn't there. "Maybe it's in the cosmetics department?" I thought, and went to the cosmetics department, but it still wasn't there. I was confused. Didn't the advertisement say that the China National Products Company was selling it? And it's a national product, the national products company should sell it, why isn't it there? Later, I asked the person in charge of the company, and found out that it was sold in the "pharmaceuticals department," so I went straight to the pharmaceuticals department.

In the glass cabinet of the pharmaceuticals department, rows of small, beautiful, flat, round boxes dazzled my eyes. The packaging was very beautiful, with a friendly purple-rose color, and a line of elegant characters in the middle, half in Western script "WindshieldA" and half in Chinese "Yun De Xiao." Next to it was a price card with a few rounded characters: "50 cents per box."

"Such a small box, selling for 50 cents, that's so expensive!" As I thought this, my forward-rushing body seemed to be retreating. However, I seemed to hear a clear voice: "Useless rouge and powder cost more than 50 cents." This voice gave me great courage, and I bought a box without hesitation.

After returning home, needless to say, I was eager to open it and try it out. However, I was too careless. It turned out to be a powder with a slightly blue tint. I opened it at an angle, so when I opened it, the powder scattered everywhere. I quickly put it down flat, but much had already been wasted. After opening the box, I followed the instructions and first wiped my glasses. After wiping them, I breathed on them and, sure enough, no fog formed. I was delighted.

"Wang Ma! Wang Ma!" I called out in a joyful voice. Wang Ma came in and, seeing me acting like a madwoman, was stunned. I instructed Wang Ma on how to use "Yun De Xiao" to wipe the mirror. She did as I said, brought a basin of wash water and tried it on the dressing table. Wang Ma was also so happy that she almost went crazy.

It has been more than half a month since then. I live in a happy mood every day. From then on, I am no longer troubled by the fog that has been bothering me all year round, and Wang Ma also seems to have much more free time.

Do you think this national product should be introduced? I say not only should it be introduced, but it should also be promoted. However, one thing I want to ask the Tiangong Industrial Company, the inventor of this national product, to pay attention to is that the box should be improved, otherwise, first-time buyers will definitely suffer losses. It is a pity to waste such a useful national product!

Ladies, Have You Forgotten? 253

— Qiacheng

Ladies, have you forgotten our painful January 28th Memorial?

Two years ago, when cannons, airplanes, warships, and the Japanese army and navy launched a major offensive against Shanghai, what was the situation in Shanghai under the cover of gunfire and flames? Now, the scars have not healed, and the great revenge has not been avenged. Although the sound of cannons seems to have faded away, the broken walls and ruins of Zhabei, Wusong, Dachang, and Zhenru remind us that the events of the past are still vivid.

You must remember this. In addition to the stories of the National Army's resistance, there were also many scenes of women being humiliated and children being massacred. At that time, whether they were victims or residents thousands of miles away, everyone was aroused with an indomitable national consciousness. Not only did they destroy their homes to relieve the national crisis as a temporary measure, but they also had the greatest determination to revive the Chinese nation and take on their responsibilities, sacrificing and fighting for themselves and the community!

Therefore, even the British "gentlemen" who looked down on the Chinese the most would say in their writings and newspapers: "In essence, the January 28th Incident was a victory for China!" This is not a self-serving facade, because the greatest gain at that time was our determination, which was a success that could not be achieved in the various traumas of the past century.

The most obvious is the vigorous and continuous national products movement that swept the country. This was also a result of the January 28th Incident. It was also a concrete manifestation of our greatest determination. It was precisely to revive the Chinese nation, especially to consolidate our own national capital, and to avoid the problem of fueling the enemy from a position of self-defense and protection.

However, the second anniversary of the January 28th Incident has passed, and the expression of that greatest determination has gradually cooled down from its initial fervor. Although beautiful people always blame others for major mistakes, the crime of negligence must still be shared by each of us. The most powerful proof is the large increase in the import of inferior goods. After being punched by others, we greet them with a smile and allow them to dump their goods again. Aren't we just drinking poison to quench our thirst and fueling the enemy?

Ladies, have you forgotten? Our painful January 28th Memorial!

Let me tell you, don't be glad that you survived the January 28th disaster. At a time when everyone is eager to act, if we don't save ourselves early, a disaster more painful than the January 28th Incident will happen again. I am not deliberately making alarmist statements. The facts are before us. Just explaining the two phrases "1936" and "Extraordinary Times" is enough to make us reflect on ourselves!

When I visited Mrs. Pan Gongzhan the other day, she said that the reason why women advocate for national products is to ensure that their precious children do not become slaves of a conquered nation. Her words were earnest and sincere, and truly a wake-up call for our women's circles.

Reporter, ladies, there is no mother in the world who does not love her children. For the sake of our children, mothers should make an effort. Moreover, the past is a warning, the scars have not healed, how can we abandon our sworn oaths, how can we change our greatest determination?

Ladies, have you forgotten? Our painful January 28th Memorial!

On this unfortunate anniversary of Women's National Products Year, our ladies' feelings must be particularly strong. However, empty words are ultimately useless. You reap what you sow. Heaven helps those who help themselves. Only by putting our heads down and working hard can we achieve the expected success.

Let's not fail the January 28th Memorial!

Let's not fail Women's National Products Year!

A Gentle Inquiry 254

— Li Anfu

Many people say: The use of national products by women is like a Buddhist grandmother pretending to eat vegetarian food; when the Women's National Products Exhibition or National Products Entertainment Fair is held, they have to respond like a Buddhist grandmother encountering the birthday of the Goddess of Mercy. This is naturally an overstatement, but I hope that the women of the future will not actually be said to be like that.

Last year was National Products Year, but according to customs reports, the number of imported foreign goods actually increased compared to the previous year; therefore, some people suggested that next year should be Foreign Goods Year, saying that maybe national products could be sold well instead. Because it is said that Chinese people often like to go in the opposite direction.

Practical experience shows: When you go to a fabric store to buy clothing material and cannot tell whether it is a national product or a foreign product, you only need to gently ask the clerk, who will then assume that you like to use foreign products, and he will tell you what kind of product it is. This is the most accurate guidance.

Domestic Glycerin 255

— Xinsheng

Glycerin, commonly known as "yangmi" (foreign honey), has many uses. It is needed in the manufacture of pharmaceuticals, cosmetics, cigarettes, canned foods, printing inks, and other industries. It is also an important material for the manufacture of explosives. Because it is related to national defense, all independent countries have factories to manufacture it themselves; however, no one in our country has ever manufactured it.

Recently, the Wuzhou Pharmacy established a second factory, purchased new machinery, and hired specialized personnel to create domestic glycerin. This is truly a somewhat satisfactory event in the National Products Year! However, starting a business is not easy. You have to work hard in the present and also consider the future. Xiang Shengwu, the current general manager of Wuzhou, said in a speech: "The manufacture of glycerin originally utilized waste materials from soap making, but the reason we are now establishing a new factory is that we have seen the ruthless bombs of the January 28th Incident destroy the essence of Zhabei. Therefore, we are now manufacturing glycerin and do not dare to establish factories in one place. If one factory is destroyed, there will still be remnants, and the foundation will not be completely destroyed." How painful are these words!

Regarding the situation of Wuzhou's manufacturing of glycerin, the Shanghai reporter group has already visited and has made satisfactory and detailed reports in various newspapers; I will not talk more about it here. I heard that the first domestic glycerin to be produced has been decided to use the "Planet" brand trademark and will be officially launched soon, and will definitely be well received by industries and businesses across the country. The types currently being investigated are as follows:

No. 1 (Double Distilled) CP Pharmaceutical Grade Specific Gravity 1.26

No. 2 (Double Distilled Decolored) Tech Industrial Grade Specific Gravity 1.26

No. 3 (Single Distilled Non-Decolored) Tech Industrial Grade Specific Gravity 1.26
